  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText16688644512202326178" style="display:none">In Allison Sekemoto's world, there is one rule left: Blood calls to blood <br /><br />She has done the unthinkable: died so that she might continue to live. Cast out of Eden and separated from the boy she dared to love, Allie will follow the call of blood to save her creator, Kanin, from the psychotic vampire Sarren. But when the trail leads to Allie's birthplace in New Covington, what Allie finds there will change the world forever—and possibly end human and vampire existence. <br /><br />There's a new plague on the rise, a strain of the Red Lung virus that wiped out most of humanity generations ago—and this strain is deadly to humans and vampires alike. The only hope for a cure lies in the secrets Kanin carries, if Allie can get to him in time. <br /><br />Allison thought that immortality was forever. But now, with eternity itself hanging in the balance, the lines between human and monster will blur even further, and Allie must face another choice she could never have imagined having to make.</span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536035536" />
    <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy"><img alt="Kat Kennedy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537750381p2/3270188.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536035536?book_show_action=true">Feb 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat Kennedy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat Kennedy" href="/user/show/3270188-kat-kennedy">Kat Kennedy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=kat-s-book-reviews">kat-s-book-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=ya-pnr-maddness">ya-pnr-maddness</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=fun-fantasy">fun-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3270188-kat-kennedy?shelf=leaves-awesomeness-behind">leaves-awesomeness-behind</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536035536" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4230047199493813205">I’m not sure how to proceed with this review WITHOUT resorting to a shit ton of gifs. I just really feel like some kind of crazy wild action would better represent how I feel than words ever could.<br/><br/>I mean, I could say that The Eternity Cure is one badass tale that left me desperate for more because this story was fucking awesome. Or I could just do this:<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/637155.gif' alt='shocked with awe' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Which is, no joke, my exact facial expression upon finishing this book. I think it actually stayed like that for a full two minutes.<br/><br/>I could tell </span>
  <span id="freeText4230047199493813205" style="display:none">I’m not sure how to proceed with this review WITHOUT resorting to a shit ton of gifs. I just really feel like some kind of crazy wild action would better represent how I feel than words ever could.<br><br>I mean, I could say that The Eternity Cure is one badass tale that left me desperate for more because this story was fucking awesome. Or I could just do this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/637155.gif" alt="shocked with awe" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Which is, no joke, my exact facial expression upon finishing this book. I think it actually stayed like that for a full two minutes.<br><br>I could tell you that Allison Sekemoto was such an unmitigated badass that I am prepared to lay my sword down at her badass feet and swear my fealty to her as the god of badass forever. Or I could just do this:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380409615ra/802098.gif" alt="I love you" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>See how much easier that is? I can’t write this bloody review because I’m too busy stalking Julie Kagawa and thinking of ways to beg her to hurry up and give me the next book. I need it. Seriously. And I can’t even talk about this book much, because I don’t want to spoil anyone. But I will let you know some vague things that you can expect:<br><br>1) Allison Sekemoto continues to be a stone-cold, kick-ass, awesomely awesome protagonist.<br><br>2) There are smoochies.<br><br>3) Things need to be killed and Allison is exactly the person to do it.<br><br>4) This is a creepy fucking book and I still shiver occasionally when thinking about it.<br><br>5) Some people in the book are horrifically horrible and terrifying.<br><br>6) Some people in this book are kind of sweet and make me smile.<br><br>7) Kanin &lt;3<br><br>8) There is a return of a character I didn’t expect and he was fuckin’ ACE, man.<br><br>9) Be prepared to want to have everyone’s babies. Just everyone’s.<br><br>10) Read it. That is all.<br><br>I have to admit, like The Immortal Rules, it started out a little slow. Allison’s naivete and willingness to trust scumbags annoyed me. However, it didn’t take long before I fully endorsed pretty much each and every decision she made. She’s just so… cool. Kagawa throws the readers right back into this creepy, desolate, and somewhat hopeless world. But somehow, when the characters in this book teamed up ready to go kick ass, I just felt this rightness. Like, “Hell yeah! It’s ASS kicking time!” For those who don’t know, ass kicking time comes right after Balls-to-the-wall crazy time, and briefly before Cleaning-blood-out-of-your-clothes time.<br><br>And Read-The-Eternity-Cure time is now, folks.<br><br>This review can also be found on my blog, <a href="http://cuddlebuggery.com/blog/2013/03/27/review-the-eternity-cure-by-julie-kagawa/" rel="nofollow noopener">Cuddlebuggery Book Blog.</a></span>

<div id="review_548465496" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/548465496" />
    <a title="Emily May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may"><img alt="Emily May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528390751p2/4622890.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548465496?book_show_action=true">Feb 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Emily May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Emily May" href="/user/show/4622890-emily-may">Emily May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4622890-emily-may?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548465496" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16518346031233070747"><a href='http://thebookgeek.co.uk' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379777457i/368079.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>"I smelled blood as soon as I walked into the room..."</b><br/><br/>And with that line begins one of the most enthralling, bloody, violent and emotional books I've read in a long time. For a book that is a combination of two of the most over-saturated young adult genres - dystopian and vampire-centric urban fantasy - this is a story which feels completely original in its execution and is utterly captivating from its grisly opening to its jaw-dropping climax. If, like me, you weren't sure about <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10215349.The_Immortal_Rules__Blood_of_Eden___1_' title='The Immortal Rules (Blood of Eden, #1) by Julie Kagawa' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Immorta</a></span>
  <span id="freeText16518346031233070747" style="display:none"><a href="http://thebookgeek.co.uk" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379777457i/368079.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>"I smelled blood as soon as I walked into the room..."</b><br><br>And with that line begins one of the most enthralling, bloody, violent and emotional books I've read in a long time. For a book that is a combination of two of the most over-saturated young adult genres - dystopian and vampire-centric urban fantasy - this is a story which feels completely original in its execution and is utterly captivating from its grisly opening to its jaw-dropping climax. If, like me, you weren't sure about <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10215349.The_Immortal_Rules__Blood_of_Eden___1_" title="The Immortal Rules (Blood of Eden, #1) by Julie Kagawa" rel="nofollow noopener">The Immortal Rules</a> and are maybe hesitant about starting this second installment: have no fear. This sequel is better in every way.<br><br>The complex character development in this sequel meant my emotions were dragged all over the place. I worried about the fate of all the main characters and loved the new directions relationships took. The most surprising character in this novel was Jackal - who at first I had to remind myself of by doing a quick scan of the previous book - his character is much more thoroughly explored in this book, he offers some much-needed comic relief in this otherwise very dark story. Let's just say I will definitely remember him from now on. <br><br>I also found myself loving and caring about Kanin and Zeke so much more in this than in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10215349.The_Immortal_Rules__Blood_of_Eden___1_" title="The Immortal Rules (Blood of Eden, #1) by Julie Kagawa" rel="nofollow noopener">The Immortal Rules</a>. Their relationships with Allison are each taken to the next level in their own way and there are parts of this novel featuring both of them which are truly heartbreaking. I have to say, Kagawa must be one of very few authors who can successfully write a relationship between a human and a vampire without resorting to misogyny. I'm fast becoming a huge fan of hers.<br><br>The story here picks up some months after the end of the last book with Allison following the call of her sire - Kanin - who has been captured and tortured by a psychotic vampire called Sarren. Forming a reluctant partnership with Jackal, Allison sets out to rescue Kanin, unsure if she'll find something that can be saved when she gets there. Along the way, Allison also discovers that the Red Lung virus has mutated and is now a threat to humans and vampires alike. The book is full of twists, turns and surprises. Kagawa isn't afraid to put her characters through several levels of hell and this serves to heighten the tension because you can never be sure whether she'll be evil enough to go there. And she usually is.<br><br>The ending left me breathless, teary-eyed and majorly annoyed. Annoyed because I've got so long to wait for the third book. Oh my god. What do I follow a book like this with?</span>
  <a data-text-id="16518346031233070747" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer517451686" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16065932295406090129"><b>I thought that I was obsessed with Jackal after the first book. Well, if that was an obsession, I don't know what is it now!</b><br/><br/>4/5⭐<br/><br/>So, a couple of notes:<br/><br/>-I think that this one was better than the previous one. Especially the beginning was very strong. <br/>-First hundred something pages I could not stop grinning but then chapter 8 came, and it went downhill. <br/>-I love Jackal even more than in the previous book. <br/>-Jackal and Allison have amazing dynamics between them. So much fun. <br/>-Where I was so happy that</span>
  <span id="freeText16065932295406090129" style="display:none"><b>I thought that I was obsessed with Jackal after the first book. Well, if that was an obsession, I don't know what is it now!</b><br /><br />4/5⭐<br /><br />So, a couple of notes:<br /><br />-I think that this one was better than the previous one. Especially the beginning was very strong. <br />-First hundred something pages I could not stop grinning but then chapter 8 came, and it went downhill. <br />-I love Jackal even more than in the previous book. <br />-Jackal and Allison have amazing dynamics between them. So much fun. <br />-Where I was so happy that Zeke was nowhere to be seen when the book started, I was certainly unhappy when he showed up. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[And it seems a bit like deus ex machina that all of them suddenly went to the exact same city. Or that Zeke even knew where the city was. And honestly? There was nothing that would even hint that Allison was going there! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />-Where there was a lot of action when it was only Jackal and Allison with Zeke it turned into a talk show. They are in the middle of danger but he needed to talk!<br />-Stick did not deserve any better; he is a coward and backstabber. <br />-The whole "cure" thing seems to be a bit confusing, hopefully, it will be explained in the next book, cause I don't buy it. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Also them not giving the cure blood to Jackal is a pretty awful thing to do. Without him, they all would be dead. Idiots. And since, I'm already in the spoiler thing; how much of the infected blood is needed to infect a vampire? Because Zeke was coughing up blood and when Allison kissed him, I would expect that she swallowed some of the blood. But then she should feel the side effects, right? Or is there some quantity? Or did the author overlook this? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />-Jackal is right, Kanin and Allison waste their time on stupid things when they have no time to waste. <br />-Is it wrong that I sort of like Sarren? He's the type of a villain I love. <br />-And I knew that the end was too good to be true... And the Epilogue had to give it away. I want to scream because that would be the best plot twist in a long time! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sorry, I really don't like Zeke, and I got a bit too excited when I thought he was killed. But now I wonder if he may be the cure for the rabidism, he has the cure for the Red Lung virus which was now mixed with him being a vampire.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><i>"And here I almost thought you weren't a complete bastard."<br /><br />"Well, that's your mistake, not mine." </i></span>

<div id="review_308846479" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/308846479" />
    <a title="Isabella" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604861-isabella"><img alt="Isabella" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1361023914p2/5604861.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/308846479?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Isabella" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Isabella" href="/user/show/5604861-isabella">Isabella</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604861-isabella?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604861-isabella?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer308846479" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5410849509746950769"><b>
  <i>"I don't believe in fate," he said carefully, "but... I do believe everything happens for a reason. That there is some plan, some meaning to this darkness we live in."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Julie Kagawa, you did it again. You held my heart in your fist and masterfully let me see the lights of paradise just so you could, in the end, beautifully destroy me. You ripped my heart in tiny little pieces and I'm still here, days after ending The Eternity Cure, trying to hold on to sanity. Believe me, after what you did at</span>
  <span id="freeText5410849509746950769" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"I don't believe in fate," he said carefully, "but... I do believe everything happens for a reason. That there is some plan, some meaning to this darkness we live in."</i>
</b><br><br>Julie Kagawa, you did it again. You held my heart in your fist and masterfully let me see the lights of paradise just so you could, in the end, beautifully destroy me. You ripped my heart in tiny little pieces and I'm still here, days after ending The Eternity Cure, trying to hold on to sanity. Believe me, after what you did at the end... I'm not sure I'll be able to breath normally until I have the third book of the trilogy in my hands. I need it so bad it hurts, but I'll wait, I'll be patient and you'll let me have what I'm yearning for, right? RIGHT?<br><br>If you read The Immortal Rules than you know that we were left with an Allie starting a new quest in order to free her sire from the evil-sociopath-vampire-master Sarren, completely alone, full of sorrow for what - and who - she left behind in Eden but determined to keep her promise and find Kanin through the blood bond that she shares with him. "Blood calls blood like sirens in the night", but what when you follow the wrong path? That's what happens when Allie finds Jackal, her blood brother and rider king from the first book that will help her find their Master - at one condition that I won't spoil for you - and will go back with her to New Covington, where everything started and everything is supposed to end... where they'll find someone who shouldn't have been there at all and a city were everything is slowly dying.<br><br>The Eternity Cure confirms what I already thought while reading The Immortal Rules: right now Blood of Eden is one of the most amazing vampire series out there, and the more I get to know this post-apocalyctic world, the more I get to love these awesome characters and their stories. I feel a connection with them all thanks to Kagawa's brilliant writing and the way she pulls at my strings. She just has this way with words, and I knew even before starting reading that this book would have been good, but damn... this good? Consider me even more HOOKED than before.<br><br><i>"The requiem has started, and when the last melody plays, the only applause will be sweet, eternal silence."</i><br><br>I loved the start and what came next, the heart-pounding scenes that instantly had me, those heart-melting moments (the piano scene... SOBS, I love it so much) where I wanted nothing more than swoon and squeel like crazy, that feeling of dread when something bad happened and the only way of knowing what would be of Allie, Jackal, Kanin, Zeke - everyone, was reading, and reading, and reading... Until the end. Until that terrible, heart-shattering, sadistic, unexpected yet PERFECT ending.<br>I have to admit, I didn't really believe that The Eternity Cure would have ended with a cliffhanger (ah-ah. Silly me). Now I look back and think of how foolish I've been, how naively I kept thinking that it couldn't get any worst than The Immortal Rules, but I was wrong. I was so wrong... I just couldn't imagine what Julie Kagawa was planning for us all. She let me taste the nectar of the gods and then she stole it from me, leaving me with nothing.<br><br><i>"It's not the physical scars that are the most painful."</i><br><br>I was left numb, all my feelings drained, and I now live with the only purpose of waiting patiently...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/526111.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>"PATIENTLY"...<br><br>Eh-ehm... Like I said, with the only purpose of waiting <s>im</s>patiently until the third, dreaded book will finally be mine (and give me the damn title already).<br><br><i>"Only death will take me away from you, vampire girl."</i><br><br>Thanks to NetGalley and Harlequin Teen for providing me with an early copy of this book!<br>The Eternity Cure on my blog:<br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://fromabooklover.blogspot.it/2013/03/review-eternity-cure-by-julie-kagawa.html">http://fromabooklover.blogspot.it/201...</a><br><br><u>
  <b>Right After reading...</b>
</u><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374520ra/728650.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And yet, Julie Kagawa is still like:<br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>She masterfully let me see the lights of paradise just so she could beautifully and easily rip my heart out. All the while I was like this:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374520ra/728652.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>and...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/391500.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And she, I'm quite sure, was like this:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374520ra/728653.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>***<br>You did not, Harlequin Teen. You did not change the covers of this series.<br>YOU DID NOT.<br><br>Shame on you, I have the first one... gotta buy the new one as well.<br><br>***<br><br>2013.<br>2013.<br>2013.<br>...<br>2013!!! I.CAN'T.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380374520ra/728654.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="5410849509746950769" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_319002299" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/319002299" />
    <a title="Eve" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5675805-eve"><img alt="Eve" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1559061534p2/5675805.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/319002299?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eve" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eve" href="/user/show/5675805-eve">Eve</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5675805-eve?shelf=2013-books">2013-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer319002299" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3988890795347688215">HOLD UP.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380376072ra/730787.gif' width='200' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Um, hi, ending? Yeah? I'm a human? I have emotions? <i>Emotions</i> that have been stomped on, thrown in a garbage disposal, crushed, mangled, eaten, regurgitated, and then taped back together, but not to the point where I'm back to normal. Thank you, for that last world crushing, feels inducing, last page. That <i>last page</i> swooped down carrying relief, happiness, and feels (oh yes, the feels), but also dread and terror BECAUSE. If you read this already, you got me. Let's cry together. <br/><br/>Holy frick</span>
  <span id="freeText3988890795347688215" style="display:none">HOLD UP.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380376072ra/730787.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Um, hi, ending? Yeah? I'm a human? I have emotions? <i>Emotions</i> that have been stomped on, thrown in a garbage disposal, crushed, mangled, eaten, regurgitated, and then taped back together, but not to the point where I'm back to normal. Thank you, for that last world crushing, feels inducing, last page. That <i>last page</i> swooped down carrying relief, happiness, and feels (oh yes, the feels), but also dread and terror BECAUSE. If you read this already, you got me. Let's cry together. <br><br>Holy frick frack where to begin? This book was awesome. Allison, of course, was the ultimate heroine and <i>insanely</i> badass. <br><br>However, I was not completely captured by Kagawa's book magic until about 100 pages in, which is excusable, but still, I deducted a star. And also, it was a bit predictable at some points. Not all, just some. <br><br>But <i>holy shish kabobs</i> if I said this book didn't live up to every sky-high expectation I had for it, I'd be lying. This book was <i>packed</i> with crazy-ass twists and turns. And <i>action</i>. The characters were fantastic. Jackal, Kinan, Zeke&lt;333, and Allison are possibly one of the most entertaining, realistic, group of characters I've ever read about. The book never had a dull moment. The pacing was consistent, the storyline was gripping, and the writing was of course, Julie Kagawa. Enough said. <br><br>AND THERE WAS THE ENDING <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380742631ra/3118066.gif" width="230" height="215" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The ending of all endings. the epitome of stressful. the cause of my shattered heart. the reason for the 70 pounds of chocolate I consumed. the best and worst part of the book. but the last page, oh the last page<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380376072ra/730788.gif" width="210" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380376072ra/730789.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But NO. The whirlwind of emotions doesn't stop there. Because behold, there was AN EXCERPT FROM THE IRON TRAITOR KJANABSJHSDB<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380376072ra/730790.gif" width="200" height="215" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh books, what have you done to me.<br><br>Everything about this was great. The characters were amazing (I could literally go on and on about them for 5 pages, but I won't), the story was enthralling, and the action and adventure aspect was definitely there. The Eternity Cure, in a word, was unputdownable. I don't say that a lot, either. So. <br><br>As you can tell, I loved this, and I refuse to wait another year for the next one. I need some more <i>Blood of Eden-ness</i>, this instant!<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Until then, I will use my telepathy skills to scream at Allison "ZEKE ISN'T DEAD!" <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This book was amazing. This series is amazing. Julie Kagawa is amazing. YOU'RE AMAZING *wink* (sorry)<br><br>2014, get over here now, and bring me <i>The Forever Song</i>. <br><br>THE FOREVER SONG. COULD THERE BE A BETTER TITLE. NO. THERE COULDN'T.<br><br>Someone hug me. </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="3988890795347688215" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_308809612" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/308809612" />
    <a title="shady boots" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4972138-shady-boots"><img alt="shady boots" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1592459241p2/4972138.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/308809612?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="shady boots" class="user" itemprop="url" name="shady boots" href="/user/show/4972138-shady-boots">shady boots</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=heroes-i-adore">heroes-i-adore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=2013-faves">2013-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=all-time-faves">all-time-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=covergasm">covergasm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=heroines-i-adore">heroines-i-adore</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4972138-shady-boots?shelf=i-just-have-a-lot-of-feelings">i-just-have-a-lot-of-feelings</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer308809612" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3258854416965417867">Julie. Oh, Julie. I love you so much.<br/><br/>But you tore my heart to pieces, Ms. Thing. ._.<br/><br/>This was everything I wanted in a sequel. It had action, it had emotion, it had character development, it had plot development, it had everything that I needed.<br/><br/>The story continues with Allison still on the search for Kanin, who's being held hostage and tortured by Sarren, a psychotic vampire. The trail leads to Allison stumbling upon Jackal, however, her blood brother, and the two form an unlikely alliance to sea</span>
  <span id="freeText3258854416965417867" style="display:none">Julie. Oh, Julie. I love you so much.<br /><br />But you tore my heart to pieces, Ms. Thing. ._.<br /><br />This was everything I wanted in a sequel. It had action, it had emotion, it had character development, it had plot development, it had everything that I needed.<br /><br />The story continues with Allison still on the search for Kanin, who's being held hostage and tortured by Sarren, a psychotic vampire. The trail leads to Allison stumbling upon Jackal, however, her blood brother, and the two form an unlikely alliance to search for their sire. Along the way she discovers that the Red Lung virus is spreading once more, a new type that's even more deadly than ever, and they must find a cure before it's too late.<br /><br />I'm probably going to spend most of this review talking about the characters, because I love them so damn much.<br /><br />Allison is one badass bitch. I'm not just saying that because she can work that katana—even though that is part of it—but I also just love her as a person. In this book we get to see more of the "demon" inside her, and how she learns to fight it back, and we get to see those scenes where she's <i>really</i> trying to hold herself back from just losing it and ripping people's throats.<br /><br />And then there's Jackal. I'll be honest, starting this book, I didn't even remember who he was, lol. But eventually my memory was refreshed. This guy was like a twisted, heartless version of Puck from <i>Iron Fey</i>. He gave the book a . . . lighter side, if you will. He had that really sarcastic, jackass kind of humor that was also pretty sadistic, too. I don't know if he showed much of that humor in the first book, because honestly, he wasn't that memorable to me. But he's definitely memorable in this one.<br /><br />I loved Kanin to pieces. I loved Zeke to pieces. I think I don't have to elaborate any further on that.<br /><br />Oh, and guess who returns in the book? Stick! This time he's working for the Prince of New Covington, and he's basically drunk with power. Poor thing tried so hard to impress and intimidate Allison. I loved that he was still the guy we used to know in the first book, but this time he has the upper hand at something and wants to rub it in Allison's face any chance he gets. But of course, he cowers in fear at just the slightest hint of her baring her fangs at him. He's different, but yet still the same.<br /><br />And finally, there's Sarren. Dear sweet lord, this man was horrifying. Probably one of the scariest villains I've ever seen, period. Not only is he evil, but he is <i>insane</i>. No I'm serious, he is completely nuts. The things he said just gave me chills, and even though I couldn't hear his voice, I could imagine it in my mind. I mean, for example: "<i>Perhaps, I will pluck out both your eyes, then remove all your teeth, and make a necklace from them. Or maybe a wind chime. I do love wind chimes, don't you, little bird?</i>" Can someone say NIGHTMARES? God, this guy is terrifying, and I love it.<br /><br />But besides the characters, I also love that the plot flowed pretty well. There was so much action, which I was just <i>living</i> for. And then the end came and Julie just threw my heart into a shredder. And threw the shredded pieces into the shredder as well afterwards. And the very final scene had me almost crying out in agony because I want the third book so bad.<br /><br />Overall I thought this was the action-packed, heart-wrenching sequel that I needed. And Julie, if you're reading this, you know I love you, girl. I absolutely adore you. But . . . please don't do that again. ._. I still haven't fully recovered yet.<br /><br />Billions of thank you's to NetGalley and Harlequin for sending me this galley!</span>
  <a data-text-id="3258854416965417867" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_458427357" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458427357" />
    <a title="Ari" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3564852-ari"><img alt="Ari" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451393828p2/3564852.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/458427357?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ari" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ari" href="/user/show/3564852-ari">Ari</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3564852-ari?shelf=best-of">best-of</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3564852-ari?shelf=arc-galley-or-author">arc-galley-or-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3564852-ari?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3564852-ari?shelf=rereading-material">rereading-material</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3564852-ari?shelf=laugh-aloud">laugh-aloud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3564852-ari?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458427357" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8807876151657978325">I repeat: <i> <br/>I.Do.Not.Like.Vampire.Books! </i><br/><br/><a href='http://www.readingaftermidnight.com/julie-kagawa/review-the-eternity-cure.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398022i/768744.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>And you see that rating up there?<br/>It should say 6 stars, but I don’t know where in the Fringe the last one might be. I should report it missing because in fact.. <br/>I.ADORED.THIS.BOOK!<br/><br/>After reading this story I might have left only one neuron (the others have gone looking for Eden again) and it’s a bit fuzzy around the edges, intoxicated by all these mind-blowing turnarounds. I barely got my head around one piece of information when another bomb was thrown</span>
  <span id="freeText8807876151657978325" style="display:none">I repeat: <i> <br>I.Do.Not.Like.Vampire.Books! </i><br><br><a href="http://www.readingaftermidnight.com/julie-kagawa/review-the-eternity-cure.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398022i/768744.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And you see that rating up there?<br>It should say 6 stars, but I don’t know where in the Fringe the last one might be. I should report it missing because in fact.. <br>I.ADORED.THIS.BOOK!<br><br>After reading this story I might have left only one neuron (the others have gone looking for Eden again) and it’s a bit fuzzy around the edges, intoxicated by all these mind-blowing turnarounds. I barely got my head around one piece of information when another bomb was thrown my way… I tell you, I’ve been at war with this book and it won! By far!<br><br>The damn thing blew my mind and left me not only rooting for various characters (loving them, then hating them only to love them again; laughing out loud at their outbursts only to cry later; wanting to read faster and see what will happen with them, then slower, then faster, but then wishing to never stop reading.. and so on..) but dying to know the outcome of this bloody mess. No pun intended, I swear!<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396274066i/9108998.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <i>“There are no good choices, Allison,” Kanin offered in a quiet voice. “There are only those you can live with, and those you can work to change.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Seriously, you cannot believe how much I love(d) the characters in this story. Even Jackal made my day too many times to count, really this guy had me cracking up half the book and I loved him even when I wanted to put a wooden stake through his unbeating heart, and (while we are at it) give him the beating of his life. He cannot play with my heart like that, no matter what for.<br><br>I loved the brotherly relationship he had with Allie though, I loved the teasing between them, I loved how they hated but also care for each-other. There would be a lot to talk about them but I cannot spoil anything for you. I will only tell you that Jackal is a very complex character: he is not quite good, nor that bad.. but a real vampire that knows how to survive and what decisions to make in order to keep his head on his shoulders. Of course, I might have hated him for it sometimes, but deep down I truly understand him too.<br><br>Anyways I might keep that fantasy for myself and not kicking Jackal’s cold ass if you promise to give me Stick, the dumb bastard, to tear him apart limb by limb!<br>I tell you, these vampire books are turning me into this creature I can barely recognize.. Where did this violence come from?<br>Oh wait.. I know.. From the bloody ending, that’s where!<br>There should be a rule about endings. It should be illegal to break people’s hearts like that and then leave them to wait God-knows-how-long for the next book… Illegal!<br><br>Now.. I heard people say that the book was too slow (it didn’t seem to me, the slow parts had Jackal in them and I deeply enjoyed his company), that the book was too long (please give me more to read, just 500 more pages, pretty please?), or that they didn’t quite enjoy as much as in the first book the relationship between Allie and Zeke (I tell you, they were cute! Ok, they were barely alone and there was not much loveliness between them, but things were complicated, after all she still wanted to drink him senseless and he still wanted to be a human for as long as he lived.. still I really liked how their relationship evolved).<br>Do I need to tell you that I don’t agree with those statements?<br><br>But I will tell you what <b>I liked</b>:<br><br>Allie – she is one of those female characters that doesn’t get on my nerves even when she becomes just a bit whinny. She is strong, she knows what kind of monster she wants to be and she tries hard to stay on that path.<br><br>Jackal – he is a jerk sometimes, but a funny one and I loved how honest his conversations with Allie were. They were enemies and they had to fight on the same side, but it was difficult for them to trust each-other because this was an one-time-deal: I help you and you’ll help me, then back to the beginning.<br><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396274066i/9108998.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <i>“I know you’re still awake.”<br>“Good for you. Shut up and go to sleep”<br>Another snicker. “What you have to ask yourself,” he continued, “is whether I’m the type who would stay awake long enough to kill you after you fall asleep, or if I’m an early riser who would kill you before you woke up.”<br>“If you want your head to stay on your neck, you’d better be neither.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Zeke – he was so human in his imperfections and so young in his love for Allie, but also he had changed from the last time we saw him. He has now a little past that might or might not want to share with us, and there are a few surprises on the way that might or might not break our hearts a bit.<br><br><a href="http://www.readingaftermidnight.com/julie-kagawa/review-the-eternity-cure.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398022i/768745.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Kanin – I always liked him, I was always interested in his back story, and we find a bit more about him, about why he turned Allie, about his past with his other ‘son’, about the virus and his part in it, about his remorses and about how he is a different kind of monster as well.<br><br>There were many other things I loved about this book, because every time I thought that the storyline became a bit predictable, everything changed completely and I was left in awe wondering “what in the world did that just happen?”. It was crazy like that and I must confess that I love craziness every now and then.<br><br>There is one more thing I want to tell you about this story, and hear me well:<br>If something seems too good to be true, remember: It is not good at all! Run like Hell and don’t look back!<br><br>Happy midnight reading!<br><a href="http://www.readingaftermidnight.com/julie-kagawa/review-the-eternity-cure.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380334106i/693595.jpg" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i> * This review can also be found at <a title="ReadingAfterMidnight" href="http://www.readingaftermidnight.com/julie-kagawa/review-the-eternity-cure.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">ReadingAfterMidnight.com</a> </i><br><i> ** ARC kindly provided by the publisher for review. Thank you so very much!</i><br>____________________________________________<br><br><a href="http://www.readingaftermidnight.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog (EN)</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingaftermidnight" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/lil_aree" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://readingaftermidnight.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> |<a href="http://www.bloglovin.com/en/blog/3285482/reading-after-midnight/" rel="nofollow noopener"> Bloglovin'</a> | <a href="http://ro.readingaftermidnight.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog (RO)</a><br>____________________________________________<br><br>Side-note:<br>Oh boy, there are just waaaaaaaay too many animated GIFs on the reviews page, LOL!<br></span>

<div id="review_1230131130" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230131130" />
    <a title="Penny" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7463065-penny"><img alt="Penny" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420145167p2/7463065.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1230131130?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Penny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Penny" href="/user/show/7463065-penny">Penny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=likereviews">likereviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7463065-penny?shelf=y-read-young-adults-fantasy">y-read-young-adults-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1230131130" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16211055383758831635">Rating Clarification: <b>3.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Before I start with the glum and doom I need to say that <b>THIS SERIES IS AWESOME AND NEEDS TO BE READ</b>.<br/><br/><b>The first book of the <i>Blood of Eden</i> series was such a phenomenal start</b> that I knew keeping up that standard was going to be tough, but I was so excited about how much I loved it that I was expecting even better for this next installment. <br/><br/>However, <b>I was a bit disappointed</b>. I didn't enjoy <i>The Eternity Cure</i> nearly as much as I did <i> <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1228896866?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Immortal Rules</a> </i>. I found that All</span>
  <span id="freeText16211055383758831635" style="display:none">Rating Clarification: <b>3.5 stars</b><br /><br />Before I start with the glum and doom I need to say that <b>THIS SERIES IS AWESOME AND NEEDS TO BE READ</b>.<br /><br /><b>The first book of the <i>Blood of Eden</i> series was such a phenomenal start</b> that I knew keeping up that standard was going to be tough, but I was so excited about how much I loved it that I was expecting even better for this next installment. <br /><br />However, <b>I was a bit disappointed</b>. I didn't enjoy <i>The Eternity Cure</i> nearly as much as I did <i> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1228896866?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Immortal Rules</a> </i>. I found that Allie’s intelligence and kickassery dropped some degrees, she wasn't really owning herself as a vampire and she was being really <b>slow figuring things out</b>. Then, I found the story to be <b>extremely predictable</b>, which in turn affected me while being in each scene facing the situations and conflicts; <b>I was somewhat detached</b>, and the big moments didn’t really affect me because <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I didn´t believe for a second they would actually be a big deal in the future, example:<br /><br /> 1)	<u>Kanin was infected</u>, had 3 days left to live, but I never believed for a second that he wasn´t going to be cured, so I wasn’t rattle.<br /> 2)	<u>Zeke was infected</u>, he was dying yet I didn´t find that emotionally moving as it should have been because again, I didn’t believe for an instant that he was going to die.<br /> 3)	<u>Zeke was kidnap and tortured and killed</u>, again It didn´t affect me, I just didn’t believe he was going to die or that he actually died, to me the worst thing that could have happened to him it would have been Zeke being turned into a vampire, but not dying, so again, I wasn´t as emotionally invested as I should have been. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>The predictability was a real letdown for me</b>, instead of being in constant tension and fascinated wondering what was going to happen next as I was while reading the first installment, here in <i>The Eternity Cure</i> I was constantly several steps ahead (sometimes way way ahead) and repeatedly predicting and being 100% right about what was coming, which was a huge discouragement.<br /><br />However, I do understand that people could have found the book <b>heart wrenching</b> if while reading it they actually believed what was happening and thought that the characters could die, then it would have been emotionally gripping. <u>Unfortunately for me I didn’t</u>. <br /><br />Other Issues:<br />1)	Repeatedly we find that in the middle of death or life situations the characters <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ yell the name of the bad guy or say something to him to attract his attention and then shoot him, as a result the bad guy doesn’t die and escape again and again. Why do they do this instead of shoot him dead while he is distracted  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> is beyond me seriously, just like in a bad movie, incredibly disappointing.<br />2)	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[The not saying I love you when is obvious Zeke wants to bothers me, and the postponing sex for a better time irritates me. Well I am sorry, but that kind of thing pisses me off, really what “better time”? They are in constant peril, the can die at any second! In what world is he living? He literally almost just died! I just don’t buy it, another thing would be if they were not ready but it seems they both are so that procrastinating is absurd and just to prolong the romance tension,  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <u>it has no realistic purpose</u>. I don’t agree with that kind of methods to achieve an interesting love story, it makes me mad.<br /><br /><b>Audiobook</b>  The narrator <b>Therese Plummer</b> does a <u>terrific job</u>. She gives the perfect tone and <u>strength</u> to the story and the characters. She unquestionably <u>improves the narrative</u>. I <u>definitely recommend listening</u> to this audio-book edition instead of reading the book. <br /><br />Overall I was entertained of coursed, and <b>I do love the universe, the story and the characters</b>, so I am truly confuse about what rating to give it. I can go anywhere from 2 to 4 stars really. I’ll decide once I finish the series, I’ll go with my general feelings.<br /><br /><br />My Reviews in the <u>Blood of Eden</u> Series:<br />Book 0.5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1229029317" rel="nofollow noopener">Dawn of Eden</a><br />Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1228896866?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Immortal Rules</a><br />Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230131130" rel="nofollow noopener">Eternity Cure</a><br />Book 2.5: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230131614?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Zeke's Letter to Allie</a> <br />Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1230131438?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">The Forever Song</a></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1709943130" />
    <a title="Sofii♡ (A Book. A Thought.)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought"><img alt="Sofii♡ (A Book. A Thought.)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1599560922p2/50405799.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1709943130?book_show_action=true">Jul 26, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sofii♡ (A Book. A Thought.)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sofii♡ (A Book. A Thought.)" href="/user/show/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought">Sofii♡ (A Book. A Thought.)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/50405799-sofii-a-book-a-thought?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1709943130" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1661752049932455620"><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“There are no good choices, Allison,' Kanin offered in a quiet voice. 'There are only those you can live with, and those you can work to change.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423715663ra/13662478.gif' width='500' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><u>Not many times happens to me, but this time I had to wait a while to process everything that had happened and put my thoughts in order so I hope can write a decent review, here I go :)</u><br/><br/><br/>When I finished the first book, literally I went immediately for the next one,I was excited to see how the story would continue , and to be honest my expectat</span>
  <span id="freeText1661752049932455620" style="display:none"><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“There are no good choices, Allison,' Kanin offered in a quiet voice. 'There are only those you can live with, and those you can work to change.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1423715663ra/13662478.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>Not many times happens to me, but this time I had to wait a while to process everything that had happened and put my thoughts in order so I hope can write a decent review, here I go :)</u><br><br><br>When I finished the first book, literally I went immediately for the next one,I was excited to see how the story would continue , and to be honest my expectations were very high, while the second books in the trilogies aren't always the best really expect much from this and guess what?!, well, this one almost completely fulfilled my expectations !.<br><br><br>In <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13581990.The_Eternity_Cure__Blood_of_Eden___2_" title="The Eternity Cure (Blood of Eden, #2) by Julie Kagawa" rel="nofollow noopener">The Eternity Cure</a> we find a much more mature <i>
  <b>Allie</b>
</i>, prepared to face this apocalyptic world that Kagawa was able to create so well, We see her more rude and much more comfortable in her vampire body , and this, in fact, is one of the points that more I liked about this book. I enjoyed a lot of action scenes where Allie looks so incredible !, although you can see that it continues her struggle against her internal demon and vampire she wants to be, I think the result is fantastic,<u>this is certainly an incredible main character, which makes me feel very pleased and achieves high-impact scenes which you can't stop reading.</u>#BADASSGIRL!<br><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470092136ra/19887548.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Jackal</b>
</i> has been a great revelation to me, is a super interesting character who brings humor and the best dialogues that this book has. I did not expect to feel so attached to him, but he has earned my respect even though his so particular methods haha, I don't want to talk much about him, because he is an amazing character and you know, Spoilers !. I can say that this character will test you and has made me want to kill him sometimes, but I love him so much!<br>He is the typical sexy vampire which is so bad, you know , but there is much more you can see in this book about him , and perhaps, <u>I hope, much more Jackal in the last one:)</u><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>I almost died when everything seemed that Jackal had betrayed to the others, OMG! false alarm Thanks God, he became on one of my favorite characters, I hope he continues on the path of good LOL, just a little bit xD</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“I sheathed my blade and glared at him. "And here I almost thought you weren't a complete bastard."<br><br>"Well, that's your mistake, not mine.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470092527ra/19887570.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Kanin</b>
</i> continue to hold his post of best character in this trilogy, I love him so much !. So much suffering for Kanin in this book, there are many things to discover about his past and one that we know that will make us understand why his actions and why so much hate from another vampires. To my, Kanin never fails at any time to be an extremely important figure in the history, his relationship with Allie has grown a lot and I was delighted to see each of their moments together, I think they have come to love and care each other as a family and that sort of tie they share is one of the sweetest things in such a dark world.<u>He has never ceased to bring you mystery and suspense to the plot, a very strong character and without doubt one of the most human, even though he is a vampire :) lol.</u> <b>#TEAMKANIN!</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1409188745ra/10946045.gif" width="500" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“Kanin peered down at me, his impassive gaze softening just a touch. "I am no longer your teacher, Allison," he said quietly. "You have been one of us for a while now. You have hunted, and you have killed. It is not my responsibility to curb you demon." He glanced past me to the place Stick and the men had stood moments before. "And I wanted to see what type of monster you had become.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><br>I have to admit that <i>
  <b>Zeke</b>
</i> has surprised me this time, it was a real surprise since its appearance in the plot, which is quite unexpected, I think he has grown a lot as a person, and no doubt it has brought enough more personality this time, it was nice read it, I enjoyed it. On the other hand I also think I'm not even sure about his relationship with Allie and as always they are kissing each other in the most wrong places! OMG guys, sometimes just is not the time. That has irritated me a bit lol.However , I must admit the growth of the character and I was happy to read about him again :) :).<br><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>I still can't get over that end, guys! !. OMG OMG!. I think the Zeke's "death" will change and come back even more badass to Allie and that really pleases me, although I can't wait to they re-find each other again , I have a hunch it will be awesome !, I hope.</i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>“You're still beautiful and dangerous and incredible, and I'll keep telling you that for as long as it takes you to believe it. But right now, all I want to do is kiss you, except I'm terrified that if I try you might throw me off this balcony.”</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br><br><u>So yeah, this book has delighted me and left me super excited for the final book !. I think it's a thousand times better than the first one, and keeps you on the edge of your seat throughout the reading. Highly recommended! :)</u><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_574225587" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/574225587" />
    <a title="Faye, la Patata" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7650833-faye-la-patata"><img alt="Faye, la Patata" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1557835753p2/7650833.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/574225587?book_show_action=true">Mar 29, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Faye, la Patata" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Faye, la Patata" href="/user/show/7650833-faye-la-patata">Faye, la Patata</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7650833-faye-la-patata?shelf=action">action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7650833-faye-la-patata?shelf=post-apocalyptic">post-apocalyptic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7650833-faye-la-patata?shelf=net-galley">net-galley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7650833-faye-la-patata?shelf=dragging">dragging</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7650833-faye-la-patata?shelf=dystopian">dystopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7650833-faye-la-patata?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7650833-faye-la-patata?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7650833-faye-la-patata?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7650833-faye-la-patata?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7650833-faye-la-patata?shelf=supernatural">supernatural</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer574225587" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13250356948799961696"><b>Final verdict: 2.5/5 but rounded up to 3<br/><br/>Disclaimer: Lots of swearing ahead. I am so sorry. I don't usually curse a lot, but this book disappointed me too much. I deserve some space to vent these feelings out.</b><br/><br/>God knows how much I detest books whose paranormal elements center around Vampires. This biased feeling of mine wasn't influenced by Twilight in any way, although that saga definitely made it worse, but I guess it's just something that stemmed from reading books that portray such creatures i</span>
  <span id="freeText13250356948799961696" style="display:none"><b>Final verdict: 2.5/5 but rounded up to 3<br /><br />Disclaimer: Lots of swearing ahead. I am so sorry. I don't usually curse a lot, but this book disappointed me too much. I deserve some space to vent these feelings out.</b><br /><br />God knows how much I detest books whose paranormal elements center around Vampires. This biased feeling of mine wasn't influenced by Twilight in any way, although that saga definitely made it worse, but I guess it's just something that stemmed from reading books that portray such creatures in a carebear manner, which is totally not cool, dude. They're supposed to be predators! They're supposed to be Rambo with sharp fangs! They're supposed to be blood-sucking, human-killing machines!<br /><br />And that is what Julie Kagawa did. She one day decided to join the Dystopian bandwagon with an all-new series and incorporated big, bad, menacing Vampires in it. And she fucking aced it in The Immortal Rules. I totally became a fan of her after that. She created a heroine whose voice was so refreshing and riveting, a world so creepy and thrilling, and a cast of Vampires who were Rambos personified. She wrote one of the best Vampire fiction out there.<br /><br />So, that brings me this question...<br /><br />Why, Julie? Why? How could you do this to your darling series?! I was expecting a book that would blow my mind away and turn my brain contents inside out, but when I turned the last page, it left only the bitter taste of disappointment and dismay in my mouth. I know; I know - I may be one of the minority here, given the number of glowing and raving reviews for this book left and right pre-publication, but... I can't. I can't lie to myself. This book bored me and infuriated me most of the time.<br /><br />Trust me. That three stars? That's my being generous already.<br /><br />Truth be told (truth accdg. to my eyes, anyway), I must say this now: this book falls short of its predecessor. Things pretty much went the wrong way for me after 20-30 or so pages... I'm not sure, but it definitely started when <b>Allison kept on talking about how she still has humanity left inside her, that Jackal is a jerk and is a sadist for embracing who he is and not denying the fact that he IS a vampire, how she'll not be a monster society expects her to become, yada yada yada... —_— All I can say is this:<br /><br /><i><u>SHUT UP, WOMAN!!!!</u></i></b><br /><br />God forbid, that was my biggest issue with this book - Allison's whines, her never-ending monologues, her being SO judgemental of other people who don't share her beliefs. It breaks my heart to see her transform from a butt-kicking, feisty individual into an angsty, whiny, annoying, stupid heroine. There are just no other words to describe her otherwise. I mean, I get it, Allison. Seriously, I do. How could I not know about your GASP! dilemmas when you keep on shoving and rubbing them on my face every 5 pages?! And it really gets old, honestly.<br /><br />I mean, how can I not be tired of reading your endless monologues of how you'll never be like cruel and blood-thirsty Jackal, that you'll always hold on to the last shreds of your humanity, that you'll never give in to your instincts, blah blah blah... FINE. I GOT IT THE FIRST TIME. It's useless to repeat it ten times over like a fucking broken record... And also, you don't want to become the monster the other Vampires are? Fine. But nobody's forcing you to become one, so how *dare* you judge others for embracing who they are, for embracing their instincts? That's like watching a lion prey on a deer and shriek how that lion was so cold-hearted because it pounced on that poor, vulnerable deer! They should love each other and make rainbows and butterflies instead!<br /><br />Oh, fucking please. Spare me the bullshitry. You're fooling no one, Allison. <br /><br />It doesn't help that the book (at least my ebook copy anyway) was a fricking 446 pages... That's a pretty big number, don't you think? Can you imagine *ME* enduring 446 pages of... of... of<b> this?!</b> It felt as if half the time Allison was going pseudo-philosophical about this bullshit, which means half the time I was either a.) bored to tears "please wake me up once the nth monologue is over, or; b.) infuriated beyond reason "whadafuck Allison fuck you die alreaddyyyy *pulls hair* *combusts*".<br /><br />The horror.<br /><br /><b>Aside from the dragging narration and the relentless whining, another problem I encountered was the sheer predictability. </b> Who the fearless leader was, the very same person who appeared in Fringe and saved the day... who the Prince's aide was... even the ending... I could see those coming a hundred miles away. I don't even need binoculars for that - it was already in my mind! All that while, I was hoping - sincerely, genuinely hoping - that Kagawa was better than those clichés I was already envisioning in my head, so just imagine my dismay when I was right on the money for each and every one of them! Each "explosive" twist, I just rolled my eyes and went, "Of course it had to be HIM... OF-FUCKING-COURSE."<br /><br />I don't know about you, but those cliché and predictable scenes? <b>Nuh-uh, not for me, no siree!</b><br /><br /><b>And, oh, did I mention the romance? </b>Please do not remind of it. Before we get to how bad it was, can someone please recommend me a novel where it doesn't focus on a Vampire/Human (although we all know how that ends up in the end) relationship? I'm so tired of all the pseudo-philosophical consequences to this and the angst it carries. Anyway, the romance felt very superficial to me. It was like Zeke and Allison were competing with each other, having an invisible battle on who between them loves the other more. <br /><br /><i>No, I love you too much so I must distance myself from you! I'm a bad, dangerous Vamp! Who knows what I could do to you if I give in to the Hunger!<br /><br />What are you talking about? *I* love you that I'm willing to risk my life for you and immerse myself in an environment full of cruel, blood-sucking abominations that I sorely hate!</i><br /><br />Back and forth, back and forth... please excuse me while I yawn my heart out.<br /><br />There were other things that annoyed the hell out of me, but check out my STATUS UPDATES of this book <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/574225587" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a> to see my suffering step-by-step. <br /><br />Of course, there were cool stuff in this book, too... and these are *badum-tss!* <b>Jackal and Kanin</b>. These two saved the book for me. Jackal, the realistic and practical dude who's also witty, snarky, and amazingly intellectual. Kanin, the mysterious, wise mentor who is also a realist. These two made the reading experience so much more fulfilling, and if it weren't for them, I'd have rated this book a measly 1 star. *shakes head*<br /><br />Despite my complaints and this rather lengthy rant, I still believe that Blood of Eden is one of the best Vampire fiction out there. Totally. Hands down. I merely think that The Eternity Cure suffers from the "Middle Book Syndrome", and I am hoping that the third book will promise us (or ME!) that feeling of awesomeness that seemed to have missed me in here. Also, readers of my review, all of these arguments are subjective. If what I said do not bother you in the slightest, then you'll maybe find yourself enjoying this installment, as others have. I just have a small level of tolerance for whiny, annoying heroines and holier-than-thou attitudes. Fuck that up, you might as well have fucked up the others.<br /><br />That is all. <br /><br />*BOW*<br /><br /><i>An ARC was sent by the Publisher via NetGalley for reviewing purposes. No money or any form of transaction was exchanged.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="13250356948799961696" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
